## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start Script] --> B[Source ~/_local_set_env_vars.sh]
    B --> C[Set SPARK Environment Variables]
    C --> D[Set Cluster Configuration]
    D --> E[Set Network Ports]
    E --> F[Set Jupyter Configuration]
    F --> G[Set SPARK_MASTER_PORT to JUPYTER_PORT]
    G --> H[Echo JUPYTER_PORT to console]
    H --> I[Append JUPYTER_PORT to /var/log/jupyter.log]
    I --> J[Set PYSPARK_DRIVER_PYTHON=jupyterhub]
    J --> K[Set PYSPARK_DRIVER_PYTHON_OPTS]
    K --> L[Activate Python venv]
    L --> M[Start PySpark with Jupyter]
    M --> N[Redirect output to /var/log/jupyterhub.log]
```

    RunPySpark --> [*]
